\hypertarget{interface_thing_smart_b_l_e_manager}{}\doxysection{Thing\+Smart\+BLEManager Class Reference}
\label{interface_thing_smart_b_l_e_manager}\index{ThingSmartBLEManager@{ThingSmartBLEManager}}


\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_b_l_e_manager}{Thing\+Smart\+BLEManager}} provides methods to manage Bluetooth LE devices by using multiple functions, such as activation, device control, and OTA updates.

\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_b_l_e_manager}{Thing\+Smart\+BLEManager}} provides methods to manage Bluetooth LE devices by using multiple functions, such as activation, device control, and OTA updates. 

The types of OTA updates\+: firmware and MCU. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{x86__64-simulator_2_thing_smart_b_l_e_core_kit_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_smart_b_l_e_manager_8h_source_l00174}{174}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{x86__64-simulator_2_thing_smart_b_l_e_core_kit_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_smart_b_l_e_manager_8h_source}{Thing\+Smart\+BLEManager.\+h}}.

Sends an OTA package to update the firmware.

The values of {\ttfamily ota\+Data}, {\ttfamily ota\+Type}, and {\ttfamily ota\+Version} can be obtained from \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_firmware_upgrade_model}{Thing\+Smart\+Firmware\+Upgrade\+Model}}. You can get \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_firmware_upgrade_model}{Thing\+Smart\+Firmware\+Upgrade\+Model}} by using \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_device_aac1dc8f24cd9296a2994a5fdf3a14c34}{get\+Firmware\+Upgrade\+Info\+:failure\+: (\+Thing\+Smart\+Device)}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Your device must be connected over Bluetooth before the update.
\end{DoxyNote}
